if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '539c18ddf374c113a572875ced485e7279a66caf') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '539c18ddf374c113a572875ced485e7279a66caf') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '08af21e50871b9fc8f93b205a65dfa47a552edfe') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '539c18ddf374c113a572875ced485e7279a66caf') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '1999040bd2c92c1cbc2c6485c79cb9f4f238fd39') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '1999040bd2c92c1cbc2c6485c79cb9f4f238fd39') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'aaae6c3f95132a839d90cbc4d8cfbae30a4e1971') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '1999040bd2c92c1cbc2c6485c79cb9f4f238fd39') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != 'fbe506faa5cd1e96143b1ba8f63efa812ee8134b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'fbe506faa5cd1e96143b1ba8f63efa812ee8134b') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '7e217b9c07a16b46b076542916bd9002ca8a0b8b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'fbe506faa5cd1e96143b1ba8f63efa812ee8134b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/script.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/script.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/script.js');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/script.js') !== '72479c6e3751ce9c665025e341e16ed170d28c84') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/script.js') !== '57e202c03ba115a88a68a11b1865af2f1deaea56') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/script.js');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/script.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');

		}

			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/script.js');

}
